Source Code

These source-code files were derived from scans of the Colossus 237 (Apollo 8 Command Module) program listing from the private collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. Scanning was by Ron Burkey. Pre-existing Colossus 249 (Apollo 9 CM) source files were used as a template, and changes between Colossus 249 and Colossus 237 were manually transcribed by a team of volunteers. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 237 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS 
	BY NASA 2021111-031  1:17 AUG. 24, 1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

012952,000024: 
012953,000025:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
012954,000026:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
012955,000027:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
012956,000028:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
012957,000029: 
012958,000030:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
012959,000031: 
012960,000032:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
012961,000033:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
012962,000034:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
012963,000035:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
012964,000036:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
012965,000037:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
012966,000038:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
012967,000039:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
012968,000040:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
012969,000041: 
012970,000042:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
012971,000043:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
012972,000044:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
012973,000045:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
012974,000046:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
012975,000047:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
012976,000048: 
012977,000049: 
012978,000050:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
012979,000051: 
012980,000052:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
012981,000053:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
012982,000054:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
012983,000055:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
012984,000056:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
012985,000057:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012986,000058: 
012987,000059:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
012988,000060:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
012989,000061:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
012990,000062:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012991,000063: 
012992,000064:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
012993,000065:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
012994,000066:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
012995,000067:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
012996,000068:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012997,000069: 
012998,000070: 
012999,000071:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
013000,000072: 
013001,000073:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
013002,000074:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.

Page 301 

013004,000076:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
013005,000077:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
013006,000078:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
013007,000079:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
013008,000080:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
013009,000081:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
013010,000082:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
013011,000083:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
013012,000084:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
013013,000085:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
013014,000086:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
013015,000087: 
013016,000088:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
013017,000089:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
013018,000090:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013019,000091: 
013020,000092: 
013021,000093:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
013022,000094: 
013023,000095:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
013024,000096:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
013025,000097:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
013026,000098: 
013027,000099:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
013028,000100:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
013029,000101:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
013030,000102:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
013031,000103:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
013032,000104:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
013033,000105:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
013034,000106: 
013035,000107:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
013036,000108:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013037,000109: 
013038,000110: 
013039,000111:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
013040,000112: 
013041,000113:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
013042,000114:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
013043,000115:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
013044,000116:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
013045,000117: 
013046,000118: 
013047,000119:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
013048,000120: 
013049,000121:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
013050,000122:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
013051,000123:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
013052,000124:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
013053,000125:

Page 302 

013055,000127: 
013056,000128:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
013057,000129:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
013058,000130: 
013059,000131: 
013060,000132:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
013061,000133: 
013062,000134:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
013063,000135:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
013064,000136: 
013065,000137:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
013066,000138:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
013067,000139:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
013068,000140:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
013069,000141: 
013070,000142:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
013071,000143:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
013072,000144: 
013073,000145:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013074,000146:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
013075,000147:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013076,000148:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013077,000149: 
013078,000150:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013079,000151:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013080,000152: 
013081,000153:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013082,000154:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
013083,000155: 
013084,000156:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013085,000157: 
013086,000158:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013087,000159:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013088,000160:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
013089,000161:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013090,000162: 
013091,000163:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013092,000164:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013093,000165: 
013094,000166:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
013095,000167:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
013096,000168: 
013097,000169: 
013098,000170:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013099,000171:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013100,000172:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013101,000173: 
013102,000174: 
013103,000175:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
013104,000176: 
013105,000177:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT

Page 303 

013107,000179:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
013108,000180:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
013109,000181: 
013110,000182:                                                                                                  #                       HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
013111,000183: 
013112,000184: 
013113,000185:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
013114,000186: 
013115,000187: 
013116,000188:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013117,000189: 
013118,000190:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013119,000191:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013120,000192:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   VERB CODE
013121,000193:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   NOUN CODE
013122,000194:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
013123,000195:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
013124,000196:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
013125,000197:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013126,000198:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013127,000199:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013128,000200:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013129,000201:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013130,000202:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013131,000203:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
013132,000204:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   MODE CODE
013133,000205:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013134,000206:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013135,000207:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013136,000208:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
013137,000209:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013138,000210:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013139,000211:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013140,000212:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
013141,000213:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013142,000214:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
013143,000215:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
013144,000216:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013145,000217:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
013146,000218:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013147,000219:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
013148,000220:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013149,000221:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013150,000222:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013151,000223:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013152,000224:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013153,000225:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013154,000226: 
013155,000227: 
013156,000228:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013157,000229:

013159,000231:                                                                                                  #  DSEXIT        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
013160,000232:                                                                                                  #  EXITEM        =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
013161,000233:                                                                                                  #  BLANKRET      =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
013162,000234: 
013163,000235:                                                                                                  #  WRDRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
013164,000236:                                                                                                  #  WDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
013165,000237:                                                                                                  #  DECRET        =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
013166,000238:                                                                                                  #  21/22REG      =       INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
013167,000239: 
013168,000240:                                                                                                  #  UPDATRET      =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
013169,000241:                                                                                                  #  CHAR          =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
013170,000242:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT         =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
013171,000243:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT       =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
013172,000244: 
013173,000245:                                                                                                  #  SGNON         =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
013174,000246:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM       =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
013175,000247:                                                                                                  #  DISTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
013176,000248:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
013177,000249: 
013178,000250:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
013179,000251:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
013180,000252:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
013181,000253:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013182,000254:                                                                                                  #                                                   MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
013183,000255:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
013184,000256:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
013185,000257:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013186,000258:                                                                                                  #                                                   MUST = HITEMIN+1.
013187,000259:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
013188,000260:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
013189,000261: 
013190,000262:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
013191,000263: 
013192,000264:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET        =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
013193,000265: 
013194,000266:                                                                                                  #  WDCNT         =       DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
013195,000267:                                                                                                  #  INREL         =       DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR ( X, Y, Z, REG )
013196,000268: 
013197,000269:                                                                                                  #  DSPMMTEM      =       MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
013198,000270:                                                                                                  #  MIXBR         =       MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
013199,000271:

013223,000295:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
013224,000296:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
013225,000297:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
013226,000298:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
013227,000299:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
013228,000300:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
013229,000301:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
013230,000302:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN ONLY)
013231,000303:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013232,000304: 
013233,000305: 
013234,000306:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013235,000307: 
013236,000308:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013237,000309:                                                                                                  #  BUF, +1, +2
013238,000310:                                                                                                  #  BUF2, +1, +2
013239,000311:                                                                                                  #  MPTEMP
013240,000312:                                                                                                  #  ADDRWD
013241,000313:                                                                                                  #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013242,000314: 
013243,000315: 
013244,000316:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013245,000317: 
013246,000318:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT        ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013247,000319:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK        ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013248,000320:                                                                                                  #                                                                                  RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013249,000321:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013250,000322: 
013251,000323: 
013252,000324:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013253,000325: 
013254,000326:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP1      =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013255,000327:                                                                                                  #  DSRUPTEM      =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013256,000328:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP2      =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013257,000329:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013258,000330:

Page 306 

013260,000332:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013261,000333:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
013262,000334:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
013263,000335:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
013264,000336:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
013265,000337:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
013266,000338:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
013267,000339:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
013268,000340:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
013269,000341:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
013270,000342:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
013271,000343:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111
013272,000344: 
013273,000345: 
013274,000346:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013275,000347:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013276,000348:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
013277,000349:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013278,000350:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013279,000351:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013280,000352: 
013281,000353:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013282,000354:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
013283,000355:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
013284,000356:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
013285,000357:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
013286,000358:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
013287,000359: 
013288,000360:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013289,000361:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
013290,000362:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
013291,000363:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
013292,000364:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
013293,000365:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
013294,000366:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
013295,000367:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
013296,000368:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
013297,000369:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
013298,000370:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
013299,000371:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
013300,000372: 
013301,000373: 
013302,000374:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013303,000375: 
013304,000376:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
013305,000377:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
013306,000378:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
013307,000379:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
013308,000380:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
013309,000381:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 307 

013311,000383:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
013312,000384:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
013313,000385:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
013314,000386:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
013315,000387:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
013316,000388:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
013317,000389:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
013318,000390:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
013319,000391: 
013320,000392: 
013321,000393:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013322,000394:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
013323,000395:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
013324,000396:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
013325,000397:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
013326,000398:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
013327,000399:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
013328,000400:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
013329,000401:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
013330,000402:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
013331,000403:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
013332,000404:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
013333,000405: 
013334,000406: 
013335,000407:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013336,000408: 
013337,000409:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013338,000410:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013339,000411:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
013340,000412:

014046,001118:

Page 323 

014048,001120:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
014049,001121: 
014050,001122:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
014051,001123:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
014052,001124:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
014053,001125:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
014054,001126:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
014055,001127: 
014056,001128:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
014057,001129:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
014058,001130: 
014059,001131:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
014060,001132: 
014061,001133:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
014062,001134:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
014063,001135:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
014064,001136: 
014065,001137:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
014066,001138:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
014067,001139:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014068,001140:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
014069,001141:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014070,001142:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
014071,001143: 
014072,001144:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
014073,001145:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
014074,001146:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
014075,001147:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
014076,001148:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
014077,001149: 
014078,001150:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
014079,001151:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
014080,001152:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
014081,001153:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
014082,001154:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014083,001155:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014084,001156:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
014085,001157:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014086,001158: 
014087,001159: 
014088,001160:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014089,001161:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
014090,001162:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014091,001163: 
014092,001164: 
014093,001165:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014094,001166:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014095,001167: 
014096,001168:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014097,001169:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
014098,001170:

Page 324 

014100,001172: 
014101,001173:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY VERBS

015229,002301:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015230,002302:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015231,002303:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015232,002304:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015233,002305:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015234,002306: 
015235,002307:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
015236,002308:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015237,002309:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
015238,002310:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
015239,002311:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015240,002312:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015241,002313:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
015242,002314: 
015243,002315:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015244,002316:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015245,002317:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015246,002318: 
015247,002319:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015248,002320:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015249,002321: 
015250,002322:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015251,002323:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
015252,002324: 
015253,002325:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

015382,002454: 
015383,002455:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015384,002456:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
015385,002457:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
015386,002458: 
015387,002459:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015388,002460: 
015389,002461:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015390,002462:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015391,002463:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015392,002464: 
015393,002465:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
015394,002466:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
015395,002467:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
015396,002468:

015398,002470: 41,3344           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015399,002471: 41,3345           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015400,002472: 41,3346           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015401,002473: 41,3347           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015402,002474: 41,3350           04610                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.

Page 360 

015842,002914:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015843,002915: 
015844,002916:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015845,002917: 
015846,002918:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015847,002919:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015848,002920:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015849,002921:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015850,002922: 
015851,002923:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015852,002924:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015853,002925:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015854,002926: 
015855,002927:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015856,002928:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015857,002929:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015858,002930:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015859,002931:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015860,002932:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015861,002933:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
015862,002934:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
015863,002935:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015864,002936:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015865,002937:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015866,002938: 
015867,002939: 40,3362           44710        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015868,002940: 40,3363           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015869,002941: 40,3364           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
015870,002942: 40,3365           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015871,002943: 40,3366           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015872,002944: 40,3367           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015873,002945: 40,3370           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015874,002946: 40,3371           03400                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
015875,002947: 40,3372           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015876,002948: 40,3373           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015877,002949: 40,3374           03376                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015878,002950: 40,3375           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015879,002951: 40,3376           04574                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015880,002952: 40,3377           21176                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015881,002953: 40,3400           34714        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015882,002954: 40,3401           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015883,002955: 40,3402           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015884,002956: 40,3403           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015885,002957: 40,3404           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015886,002958: 40,3405           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015887,002959: 
015888,002960: 40,3406                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015889,002961:

Page 361 

015891,002963:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
015892,002964:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015893,002965:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015894,002966:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015895,002967:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015896,002968: 
015897,002969:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015898,002970:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015899,002971:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015900,002972: 
015901,002973:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015902,002974:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015903,002975: 
015904,002976:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015905,002977:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015906,002978:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015907,002979:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
015908,002980:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015909,002981: 
015910,002982:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015911,002983:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015912,002984:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015913,002985:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015914,002986: 
015915,002987:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015916,002988:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015917,002989:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015918,002990:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015919,002991:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015920,002992:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015921,002993:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015922,002994: 
015923,002995:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015924,002996:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015925,002997: 
015926,002998:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015927,002999:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015928,003000: 
015929,003001:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015930,003002:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015931,003003: 
015932,003004:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015933,003005:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015934,003006:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015935,003007:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015936,003008:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015937,003009:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015938,003010:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015939,003011: 
015940,003012:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 362 

015942,003014:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015943,003015:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
015944,003016:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015945,003017:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015946,003018:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
015947,003019:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015948,003020:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
015949,003021:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
015950,003022:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
015951,003023: 
015952,003024:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
015953,003025:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)

016070,003142:    4220           34674        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
